    ab.account_id,
    ci.customer_id,
 	ci.first_name,
    ci.last_name,
    SUM(th.amount) as total_amount,
    COUNT(th.transaction_id) as transaction_count

INNER JOIN

    ci.registration_date >= '2023-01-01'
GROUP BY
    ci.customer_id
HAVING
    COUNT(th.transaction_id) > 10;
